Event
.  has and belongs to many users
.  is valid with valid attributes
.  is valid without a description
.  is not valid without a name
.  is not valid without points
.  is valid with 0 points
.  is not valid with negative points
.  is not valid without a start date
.  is not valid without an end date
.  is not valid if the end date is before the start date

PointEvent
.  has and belongs to many users
.  is valid with valid attributes
.  is valid without a description
.  is not valid without a name
.  is not valid without points
.  is valid with 0 points
.  is not valid with negative points

User
.  is valid with valid attributes
.  is not valid without a email
.  is not valid without role
.  is not valid with out of range role
.  is not valid with out first name
.  is not valid with out last name
.  is not valid with out phone number
.  is not valid with out full 10 digit phone number
.  is not valid with out classification
.  is not valid with out t-shirt size
.  is not valid with out optInEmail
.  is not valid with out points
.  is not valid with negative points
.  is valid with 0 points
